# MAPSXPLR API SDK å‚è€ƒæ–‡æ¡£

## é¡¹ç›®æ¦‚è¿°

**MAPSXPLR** æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªåŸºäº Google Maps å’Œ Gemini AI çš„æ™ºèƒ½åœ°å›¾æ¢ç´¢åº”ç”¨ï¼Œæ”¯æŒä¸¤ç§æ“ä½œæ¨¡å¼ï¼šé€šç”¨æ¢ç´¢æ¨¡å¼å’Œæ—¥ç¨‹è§„åˆ’æ¨¡å¼ã€‚

- **é¡¹ç›®åç§°**: Maps Planner
- **ç‰ˆæœ¬**: v0.0.1
- **æŠ€æœ¯æ ˆ**: TypeScript + Vite + Google Maps API + Gemini AI

---

## æ ¸å¿ƒ API é›†æˆ

### 1. Google Gemini AI API

#### åˆå§‹åŒ–å®¢æˆ·ç«¯

```typescript
import {GoogleGenAI} from '@google/genai';

const ai = new GoogleGenAI({
  vertexai: false,
  apiKey: process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY,
});
```

#### æ¨¡å‹é…ç½®

- **æ¨¡å‹**: `gemini-2.5-flash`
- **æ¸©åº¦**: 1.0
- **åŠŸèƒ½å£°æ˜**: æ”¯æŒ `location` å’Œ `line` å‡½æ•°è°ƒç”¨

#### å†…å®¹ç”Ÿæˆ API

```typescript
const response = await ai.models.generateContentStream({
  model: 'gemini-2.5-flash',
  contents: finalPrompt,
  config: {
    systemInstruction: updatedInstructions,
    temperature: 1,
    tools: [{
      functionDeclarations: [
        locationFunctionDeclaration,
        lineFunctionDeclaration,
      ],
    }],
  },
});
```

### 2. Google Maps JavaScript API

#### åº“å¯¼å…¥

```typescript
const {Map} = await google.maps.importLibrary('maps');
const {LatLngBounds} = await google.maps.importLibrary('core');
const {AdvancedMarkerElement} = await google.maps.importLibrary('marker');
```

#### åœ°å›¾åˆå§‹åŒ–

```typescript
map = new Map(document.getElementById('map'), {
  center: {lat: -34.397, lng: 150.644},
  zoom: 8,
  mapId: '4504f8b37365c3d0',
  gestureHandling: 'greedy',
  // ç¦ç”¨æ‰€æœ‰é»˜è®¤æ§ä»¶
  zoomControl: false,
  cameraControl: false,
  mapTypeControl: false,
  scaleControl: false,
  streetViewControl: false,
  rotateControl: false,
  fullscreenControl: false,
});
```

## å‡½æ•°å£°æ˜ (Function Declarations)

### 1. Location å‡½æ•°å£°æ˜

ç”¨äºæå–åœ°ç†ä½ç½®æ•°æ®çš„ AI å‡½æ•°å£°æ˜ï¼š

```typescript
const locationFunctionDeclaration: FunctionDeclaration = {
  name: 'location',
  parameters: {
    type: Type.OBJECT,
    description: 'Geographic coordinates of a location.',
    properties: {
      name: {
        type: Type.STRING,
        description: 'Name of the location.',
      },
      description: {
        type: Type.STRING,
        description: 'Description of the location: why is it relevant, details to know.',
      },
      lat: {
        type: Type.STRING,
        description: 'Latitude of the location.',
      },
      lng: {
        type: Type.STRING,
        description: 'Longitude of the location.',
      },
      // æ—¥ç¨‹è§„åˆ’æ¨¡å¼ä¸“ç”¨å±æ€§
      time: {
        type: Type.STRING,
        description: 'Time of day to visit this location (e.g., "09:00", "14:30").',
      },
      duration: {
        type: Type.STRING,
        description: 'Suggested duration of stay at this location (e.g., "1 hour", "45 minutes").',
      },
      sequence: {
        type: Type.NUMBER,
        description: 'Order in the day itinerary (1 = first stop of the day).',
      },
    },
    required: ['name', 'description', 'lat', 'lng'],
  },
};
```

### 2. Line å‡½æ•°å£°æ˜

ç”¨äºæå–è·¯çº¿/è¿æ¥æ•°æ®çš„ AI å‡½æ•°å£°æ˜ï¼š

```typescript
const lineFunctionDeclaration: FunctionDeclaration = {
  name: 'line',
  parameters: {
    type: Type.OBJECT,
    description: 'Connection between a start location and an end location.',
    properties: {
      name: {
        type: Type.STRING,
        description: 'Name of the route or connection',
      },
      start: {
        type: Type.OBJECT,
        description: 'Start location of the route',
        properties: {
          lat: { type: Type.STRING, description: 'Latitude of the start location.' },
          lng: { type: Type.STRING, description: 'Longitude of the start location.' },
        },
      },
      end: {
        type: Type.OBJECT,
        description: 'End location of the route',
        properties: {
          lat: { type: Type.STRING, description: 'Latitude of the end location.' },
          lng: { type: Type.STRING, description: 'Longitude of the end location.' },
        },
      },
      // æ—¥ç¨‹è§„åˆ’æ¨¡å¼ä¸“ç”¨å±æ€§
      transport: {
        type: Type.STRING,
        description: 'Mode of transportation between locations (e.g., "walking", "driving", "public transit").',
      },
      travelTime: {
        type: Type.STRING,
        description: 'Estimated travel time between locations (e.g., "15 minutes", "1 hour").',
      },
    },
    required: ['name', 'start', 'end'],
  },
};
```

- **çˆ¶å­é€šä¿¡**: Props + Events
- **å…„å¼Ÿé€šä¿¡**: Pinia Store
- **è·¨å±‚é€šä¿¡**: äº‹ä»¶æ€»çº¿

### 3.3 æ ¸å¿ƒæ¨¡å—è®¾è®¡

#### 3.3.1 AI å¯¹è¯æ¨¡å—

```typescript
// stores/chat.ts
interface ChatMessage {
  id: string
  role: 'user' | 'assistant'
  content: string
  timestamp: Date
  functionCalls?: FunctionCall[]
}

interface FunctionCall {
  name: 'location' | 'line'
  arguments: Record<string, any>
}

class ChatStore {
  messages: ChatMessage[]
  isLoading: boolean
  
  async sendMessage(content: string): Promise<void>
  async callDeepSeekAPI(messages: ChatMessage[]): Promise<ChatMessage>
  handleFunctionCall(call: FunctionCall): void
}
```

#### 3.3.2 åœ°å›¾æ§åˆ¶æ¨¡å—

```typescript
// stores/map.ts
interface MapLocation {
  id: string
  name: string
  coordinates: [number, number]
  description: string
  category: string
  duration?: number
  sequence?: number
}

interface MapRoute {
  id: string
  from: string
  to: string
  coordinates: [number, number][]
  transport: 'walking' | 'driving' | 'transit'
  duration: number
}

class MapStore {
  locations: MapLocation[]
  routes: MapRoute[]
  selectedLocation: string | null
  
  addLocation(location: MapLocation): void
  addRoute(route: MapRoute): void
  selectLocation(id: string): void
  clearAll(): void
}
```

#### 3.3.3 è¡Œç¨‹è§„åˆ’æ¨¡å—

```typescript
// stores/timeline.ts
interface TimelineItem {
  id: string
  locationId: string
  startTime: string
  endTime: string
  duration: number
  transport?: {
    type: string
    duration: number
    to: string
  }
}

class TimelineStore {
  items: TimelineItem[]
  isVisible: boolean
  
  generateTimeline(locations: MapLocation[]): void
  updateItem(id: string, updates: Partial<TimelineItem>): void
  exportPlan(): string
}
```

### 6.2 CI/CD æµæ°´çº¿

#### GitHub Actions é…ç½®

```yaml
name: Build and Deploy

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

jobs:
  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '18'
      - run: npm ci
      - run: npm run lint
      - run: npm run test
      - run: npm run build

  deploy:
    needs: test
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '18'
      - run: npm ci
      - run: npm run build
      - uses: peaceiris/actions-gh-pages@v3
        with:
          github_token: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
          publish_dir: ./dist
```

#### éƒ¨ç½²æµç¨‹

1. **ä»£ç æäº¤**ï¼šå¼€å‘è€…æ¨é€ä»£ç åˆ° main åˆ†æ”¯
2. **è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–æµ‹è¯•**ï¼šè¿è¡Œ lintã€testã€build
3. **æ„å»ºäº§ç‰©**ï¼šç”Ÿæˆé™æ€æ–‡ä»¶åˆ° dist ç›®å½•
4. **éƒ¨ç½²å‘å¸ƒ**ï¼šè‡ªåŠ¨éƒ¨ç½²åˆ° GitHub Pages
5. **éªŒè¯ä¸Šçº¿**ï¼šè‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–éªŒè¯éƒ¨ç½²ç»“æœ

## ç¬¬11æ­¥ï¼šåˆ›å»ºæ ¸å¿ƒç»„ä»¶

åˆ›å»ºä¸»è¦çš„ Vue ç»„ä»¶ `src/components/MapExplorer.vue`ï¼š

```vue:src/components/MapExplorer.vue
<template>
  <div class="flex h-full">
    <!-- åœ°å›¾åŒºåŸŸ -->
    <div class="flex-1 relative">
      <div id="map" class="w-full h-full"></div>
      
      <!-- å¯¹è¯è¾“å…¥åŒºåŸŸ -->
      <div class="absolute bottom-4 left-4 right-4 bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-4">
        <div class="flex gap-2">
          <el-input
            v-model="userInput"
            placeholder="è¯·æè¿°æ‚¨æƒ³æ¢ç´¢çš„åœ°æ–¹æˆ–æ´»åŠ¨..."
            @keyup.enter="sendMessage"
            :loading="isLoading"
            class="flex-1"
          />
          <el-button 
            type="primary" 
            @click="sendMessage"
            :loading="isLoading"
            icon="Search"
          >
            æ¢ç´¢
          </el-button>
        </div>
        
        <div class="flex gap-2 mt-2">
          <el-button size="small" @click="setMode('explore')" :type="mode === 'explore' ? 'primary' : 'default'">
            ğŸ¯ æ¢ç´¢æ¨¡å¼
          </el-button>
          <el-button size="small" @click="setMode('plan')" :type="mode === 'plan' ? 'primary' : 'default'">
            ğŸ“… è§„åˆ’æ¨¡å¼
          </el-button>
          <el-button size="small" @click="resetMap">
            ğŸ”„ é‡ç½®
          </el-button>
          <el-button size="small" @click="exportPlan" v-if="mode === 'plan'">
            ğŸ“¤ å¯¼å‡º
          </el-button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- ä¾§è¾¹æ  -->
    <div class="w-80 bg-white border-l border-gray-200 flex flex-col">
      <!-- åœ°ç‚¹å¡ç‰‡åŒºåŸŸ -->
      <div class="flex-1 p-4 overflow-y-auto">
        <h3 class="text-lg font-semibold mb-4">æ¨èåœ°ç‚¹</h3>
        <div class="space-y-4">
          <LocationCard 
            v-for="location in locations" 
            :key="location.id"
            :location="location"
            @select="selectLocation"
          />
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <!-- æ—¶é—´çº¿é¢æ¿ -->
      <TimelinePanel 
        v-if="showTimeline && mode === 'plan'"
        :timeline="timeline"
        @close="showTimeline = false"
      />
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, onMounted } from 'vue';
import { ElInput, ElButton } from 'element-plus';
import LocationCard from './LocationCard.vue';
import TimelinePanel from './Timeline/TimelinePanel.vue';
import { useMapStore } from '../stores/map';
import { useChatStore } from '../stores/chat';

const mapStore = useMapStore();
const chatStore = useChatStore();

const userInput = ref('');
const isLoading = ref(false);
const mode = ref<'explore' | 'plan'>('explore');
const showTimeline = ref(false);

const locations = computed(() => mapStore.locations);
const timeline = computed(() => mapStore.timeline);

let map: any = null;

onMounted(() => {
  initMap();
});

const initMap = () => {
  // åˆå§‹åŒ– Leaflet åœ°å›¾
  map = L.map('map').setView([39.9042, 116.4074], 13); // åŒ—äº¬åæ ‡
  
  L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png', {
    attribution: 'Â© OpenStreetMap contributors'
  }).addTo(map);
};

const sendMessage = async () => {
  if (!userInput.value.trim() || isLoading.value) return;
  
  isLoading.value = true;
  try {
    await chatStore.sendMessage(userInput.value, mode.value);
    userInput.value = '';
    
    if (mode.value === 'plan') {
      showTimeline.value = true;
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯å¤±è´¥:', error);
  } finally {
    isLoading.value = false;
  }
};

const setMode = (newMode: 'explore' | 'plan') => {
  mode.value = newMode;
  if (newMode === 'explore') {
    showTimeline.value = false;
  }
};

const selectLocation = (locationId: string) => {
  mapStore.selectLocation(locationId);
  // åœ°å›¾å®šä½åˆ°é€‰ä¸­çš„åœ°ç‚¹
  const location = locations.value.find(l => l.id === locationId);
  if (location && map) {
    map.setView([location.coordinates[1], location.coordinates[0]], 15);
  }
};

const resetMap = () => {
  mapStore.clearAll();
  userInput.value = '';
  showTimeline.value = false;
  if (map) {
    map.setView([39.9042, 116.4074], 13);
  }
};

const exportPlan = () => {
  // å¯¼å‡ºè¡Œç¨‹è®¡åˆ’
  const planText = mapStore.exportPlan();
  const blob = new Blob([planText], { type: 'text/plain' });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = url;
  a.download = `è¡Œç¨‹è®¡åˆ’_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.txt`;
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
};
</script>
```

## ç¬¬12æ­¥ï¼šåˆ›å»ºçŠ¶æ€ç®¡ç†

åˆ›å»ºåœ°å›¾çŠ¶æ€ç®¡ç† `src/stores/map.ts`ï¼š

```typescript:src/stores/map.ts
import { defineStore } from 'pinia';

export interface MapLocation {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  coordinates: [number, number]; // [lng, lat]
  description: string;
  category: string;
  duration?: number;
  sequence?: number;
}

export interface MapRoute {
  id: string;
  from: string;
  to: string;
  coordinates: [number, number][];
  transport: 'walking' | 'driving' | 'transit';
  duration: number;
}

export interface TimelineItem {
  id: string;
  locationId: string;
  startTime: string;
  endTime: string;
  duration: number;
  transport?: {
    type: string;
    duration: number;
    to: string;
  };
}

export const useMapStore = defineStore('map', {
  state: () => ({
    locations: [] as MapLocation[],
    routes: [] as MapRoute[],
    timeline: [] as TimelineItem[],
    selectedLocation: null as string | null,
  }),
  
  actions: {
    addLocation(location: MapLocation) {
      this.locations.push(location);
    },
    
    addRoute(route: MapRoute) {
      this.routes.push(route);
    },
    
    selectLocation(id: string) {
      this.selectedLocation = id;
    },
    
    clearAll() {
      this.locations = [];
      this.routes = [];
      this.timeline = [];
      this.selectedLocation = null;
    },
    
    generateTimeline(locations: MapLocation[]) {
      // ç”Ÿæˆæ—¶é—´çº¿é€»è¾‘
      this.timeline = locations.map((location, index) => ({
        id: `timeline-${index}`,
        locationId: location.id,
        startTime: `${9 + index * 2}:00`,
        endTime: `${9 + index * 2 + 1}:30`,
        duration: 90,
        transport: index < locations.length - 1 ? {
          type: 'walking',
          duration: 15,
          to: locations[index + 1].name
        } : undefined
      }));
    },
    
    exportPlan(): string {
      let planText = '# æˆ‘çš„è¡Œç¨‹è®¡åˆ’\n\n';
      
      this.timeline.forEach((item, index) => {
        const location = this.locations.find(l => l.id === item.locationId);
        if (location) {
          planText += `## ${index + 1}. ${location.name}\n`;
          planText += `**æ—¶é—´**: ${item.startTime} - ${item.endTime}\n`;
          planText += `**æè¿°**: ${location.description}\n`;
          if (item.transport) {
            planText += `**å‰å¾€ä¸‹ä¸€ç«™**: ${item.transport.type} ${item.transport.duration}åˆ†é’Ÿ\n`;
          }
          planText += '\n';
        }
      });
      
      return planText;
    }
  }
});
```

åˆ›å»ºèŠå¤©çŠ¶æ€ç®¡ç† `src/stores/chat.ts`ï¼š

```typescript:src/stores/chat.ts
import { defineStore } from 'pinia';
import { useMapStore } from './map';

interface ChatMessage {
  id: string;
  role: 'user' | 'assistant';
  content: string;
  timestamp: Date;
}

export const useChatStore = defineStore('chat', {
  state: () => ({
    messages: [] as ChatMessage[],
    isLoading: false,
  }),
  
  actions: {
    async sendMessage(content: string, mode: 'explore' | 'plan') {
      const mapStore = useMapStore();
      
      // æ·»åŠ ç”¨æˆ·æ¶ˆæ¯
      this.messages.push({
        id: Date.now().toString(),
        role: 'user',
        content,
        timestamp: new Date()
      });
      
      this.isLoading = true;
      
      try {
        // è°ƒç”¨ DeepSeek API
        const response = await this.callDeepSeekAPI(content, mode);
        
        // æ·»åŠ  AI å›å¤
        this.messages.push({
          id: (Date.now() + 1).toString(),
          role: 'assistant',
          content: response.content,
          timestamp: new Date()
        });
        
        // å¤„ç†å‡½æ•°è°ƒç”¨
        if (response.functionCalls) {
          response.functionCalls.forEach((call: any) => {
            this.handleFunctionCall(call);
          });
        }
        
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('API è°ƒç”¨å¤±è´¥:', error);
        // æ·»åŠ é”™è¯¯æ¶ˆæ¯
        this.messages.push({
          id: (Date.now() + 2).toString(),
          role: 'assistant',
          content: 'æŠ±æ­‰ï¼Œæˆ‘é‡åˆ°äº†ä¸€äº›é—®é¢˜ã€‚è¯·ç¨åå†è¯•ã€‚',
          timestamp: new Date()
        });
      } finally {
        this.isLoading = false;
      }
    },
    
    async callDeepSeekAPI(content: string, mode: string) {
      // è¿™é‡Œéœ€è¦å®é™…çš„ DeepSeek API è°ƒç”¨
      // æš‚æ—¶è¿”å›æ¨¡æ‹Ÿæ•°æ®
      return {
        content: `æˆ‘ä¸ºæ‚¨æ‰¾åˆ°äº†ä¸€äº›${mode === 'explore' ? 'æœ‰è¶£çš„åœ°ç‚¹' : 'è¡Œç¨‹å»ºè®®'}ã€‚`,
        functionCalls: [
          {
            name: 'location',
            arguments: {
              name: 'å¤©å®‰é—¨å¹¿åœº',
              coordinates: [116.3974, 39.9069],
              description: 'ä¸­å›½çš„è±¡å¾æ€§åœ°æ ‡ï¼Œå†å²æ‚ ä¹…çš„å¹¿åœº',
              category: 'å†å²æ–‡åŒ–'
            }
          }
        ]
      };
    },
    
    handleFunctionCall(call: any) {
      const mapStore = useMapStore();
      
      if (call.name === 'location') {
        const location = {
          id: Date.now().toString(),
          name: call.arguments.name,
          coordinates: call.arguments.coordinates,
          description: call.arguments.description,
          category: call.arguments.category
        };
        mapStore.addLocation(location);
      } else if (call.name === 'line') {
        const route = {
          id: Date.now().toString(),
          from: call.arguments.from,
          to: call.arguments.to,
          coordinates: call.arguments.coordinates,
          transport: call.arguments.transport,
          duration: call.arguments.duration
        };
        mapStore.addRoute(route);
      }
    }
  }
});
```

## ç¬¬13æ­¥ï¼šåˆ›å»ºç»„ä»¶

```vue:src/components/LocationCard.vue
<template>
  <div 
    class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border border-gray-200 p-4 cursor-pointer hover:shadow-md transition-shadow"
    :class="{ 'ring-2 ring-blue-500': isSelected }"
    @click="$emit('select', location.id)"
  >
    <div class="flex items-start gap-3">
      <div class="w-12 h-12 bg-gray-200 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center">
        <i class="fas fa-map-marker-alt text-blue-500"></i>
      </div>
      
      <div class="flex-1">
        <h4 class="font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-1">{{ location.name }}</h4>
        <p class="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-2">{{ location.description }}</p>
        
        <div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-gray-500">
          <span class="bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 px-2 py-1 rounded">
            {{ location.category }}
          </span>
          <span v-if="location.duration">
            {{ location.duration }}åˆ†é’Ÿ
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>
```

åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´çº¿é¢æ¿ç»„ä»¶ `src/components/Timeline/TimelinePanel.vue`ï¼š

```vue:src/components/Timeline/TimelinePanel.vue
<template>
  <div class="bg-white border-t border-gray-200 p-4">
    <div class="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
      <h3 class="text-lg font-semibold">ğŸ“… ä»Šæ—¥è¡Œç¨‹è®¡åˆ’</h3>
      <el-button size="small" @click="$emit('close')" icon="Close" circle />
    </div>
    
    <div class="space-y-3 max-h-64 overflow-y-auto">
      <div 
        v-for="(item, index) in timeline" 
        :key="item.id"
        class="flex items-start gap-3 p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg"
      >
        <div class="w-8 h-8 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-sm font-semibold">
          {{ index + 1 }}
        </div>
        
        <div class="flex-1">
          <div class="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
            <span class="text-sm font-medium">{{ item.startTime }} - {{ item.endTime }}</span>
            <span class="text-xs text-gray-500">({{ item.duration }}åˆ†é’Ÿ)</span>
          </div>
          
          <h4 class="font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-1">
            {{ getLocationName(item.locationId) }}
          </h4>
          
          <div v-if="item.transport" class="text-xs text-gray-600 flex items-center gap-1">
            <i :class="getTransportIcon(item.transport.type)"></i>
            <span>{{ item.transport.type }} {{ item.transport.duration }}åˆ†é’Ÿ â†’ {{ item.transport.to }}</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <div class="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-gray-200">
      <div class="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-2">
        ğŸ“Š æ€»è®¡ï¼š{{ totalDuration }}å°æ—¶æ¸¸è§ˆ | ğŸš¶ é¢„ä¼°æ­¥è¡Œæ—¶é—´
      </div>
      
      <div class="flex gap-2">
        <el-button size="small" @click="exportPlan">
          ğŸ“¤ å¯¼å‡ºè®¡åˆ’
        </el-button>
        <el-button size="small">
          ğŸ”„ é‡æ–°è§„åˆ’
        </el-button>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { computed } from 'vue';
import { ElButton } from 'element-plus';
import type { TimelineItem } from '../../stores/map';
import { useMapStore } from '../../stores/map';

interface Props {
  timeline: TimelineItem[];
}

const props = defineProps<Props>();
defineEmits<{
  close: [];
}>();

const mapStore = useMapStore();

const totalDuration = computed(() => {
  const total = props.timeline.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.duration, 0);
  return (total / 60).toFixed(1);
});

const getLocationName = (locationId: string) => {
  const location = mapStore.locations.find(l => l.id === locationId);
  return location?.name || 'æœªçŸ¥åœ°ç‚¹';
};

const getTransportIcon = (transport: string) => {
  const icons = {
    walking: 'fas fa-walking',
    driving: 'fas fa-car',
    transit: 'fas fa-bus'
  };
  return icons[transport as keyof typeof icons] || 'fas fa-walking';
};

const exportPlan = () => {
  const planText = mapStore.exportPlan();
  const blob = new Blob([planText], { type: 'text/plain' });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = url;
  a.download = `è¡Œç¨‹è®¡åˆ’_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.txt`;
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
};
</script>
```
